
1. Dendritic cell response to Leishmania major infection: time course
Analysis of dendritic cells for up to 24 hours following infection with Leishmania major. Leishmaniasis is a group of insect vector transmitted parasitic diseases. Results provide insight into the molecular response of dendritic cells to L. major infections.
Organism:	Homo sapiens
Type:		Expression profiling by array, count, 2 infection, 4 time sets
Platform: GPL570 Series: GSE42088 15 Samples
FTP download: GEO (CEL) ftp://ftp.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/geo/datasets/GDS5nnn/GDS5086/
DataSet		Accession: GDS5086	ID: 5086

2. First-time acute myocardial infarction: peripheral blood
